	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'a7a1de114c3277c481af1544f8eacb7413b2ddf0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'a7a1de114c3277c481af1544f8eacb7413b2ddf0') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '8e2f3942a58c70df5e2e2bcf8aa2caf669ae6577') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'a7a1de114c3277c481af1544f8eacb7413b2ddf0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php') != 'a7441625d282b0d0d5e3cf24fe85e91518278c01') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php') !== 'a7441625d282b0d0d5e3cf24fe85e91518278c01') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php') !== '550ed6f972a9d80175f6a653de602ce06ba47155') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php') !== 'a7441625d282b0d0d5e3cf24fe85e91518278c01') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/danielmarschall/uuid_mac_utils/includes/mac_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1255\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1255') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
